  24 /* We use one big table for the mapping.  We know that the first byte
  25    is in range 0x21 to 0xea.  The second byte never is in the ranges
  26    0x00 to 0x20 and 0x7f to 0xff.  Compacting the table by excluding
  27    these ranges we get a table with only this gaps:
  28 
  29    at   0x222e  0x2241  0x2250  0x226a  0x2279  0x2321  0x2339  0x235a
  30    len  12  9   12  8   5   15  8   7
  31 
  32    at   0x237a  0x2473  0x2576  0x2638  0x2658  0x2741  0x2771  0x2840
  33    len  4   11  8   9   38  16  13  62
  34 
  35    at   0x4f53
  36    len  43
  37 
  38    It's not worth trying to use these gaps.  The table can be generated
  39    using
  40 
  41    egrep '^0x' < .../eastasia/jis/jis0208.txt |
  42    perl tab.pl
  43 
  44    with tab.pl containing:
  45    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  46    $n=0;
  47    while (<>) {
  48      local($sjis, $jis, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
  49      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
  50      local($s)=hex($jis);
  51      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 4 eq 0);
  52      ++$n;
  53      printf (" [0x%04x] = 0x%04x,",
  54          int(($s - 0x2121) / 256) * 94 + (($s - 0x2121) & 0xff), $u);
  55    }
  56    printf ("\n");
  57    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  58 */
  59 const uint16_t __jis0208_to_ucs[0x1e80] =
  60 {

1801 /* The following table can be generated using
1802 
1803    egrep '^0x' < .../eastasia/jis/jis0208.txt |
1804    awk '{ print $3, $2}' | egrep '^0x0[34]' | sort -u | perl tab.pl
1805 
1806    where tab.pl contains:
1807 
1808    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1809    $n=0;
1810    while (<>) {
1811      local($ucs4, $jis, %rest) = split;
1812      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
1813      local($s)=hex($jis);
1814      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 3 eq 0);
1815      ++$n;
1816      printf (" [0x%02x] = \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",",
1817          int(($u - 0x391) / 256) * 94 + (($u - 0x391) & 0xff),
1818          int($s/256), $s % 256);
1819    }
1820    printf ("\n");
1821    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1822 */

1865 
1866 /* The mapping of all the other UCS values is quite difficult since they
1867    are distributed from 0x2010 upto to 0xffe5.  There are many gaps with
1868    unpredictable place and size.  Therefore we use a table which maps
1869    ranges to idexes in a table.  This table ca be generated with:
1870 
1871    egrep '^0x' < .../eastasia/jis/jis0208.txt | awk '{ print $3, $2}' |
1872    egrep '^0x[^01]' | sort -u | perl tab.pl
1873 
1874    where tab.pl is
1875 
1876    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1877    $first=$last=$idx=0;
1878    while (<>) {
1879      local($ucs,$jis,%rest) = split;
1880      local($u)=hex($ucs);
1881      if ($u - $last > 6) {
1882        if ($last != 0) {
1883      printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d },\n",
1884          $first, $last, $idx);
1885      $idx += $last - $first + 1;
1886        }
1887        $first=$u;
1888      }
1889      $last=$u;
1890    }
1891    printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d }\n",
1892        $first, $last, $idx);
1893    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1894 */
1895

2609 /* The following table is indexed using the previous tables.  It is
2610    therefore indexed using UCS with leaving large gaps out.  It can
2611    be computed with
2612 
2613    egrep '^0x' < .../eastasia/jis/jis0208.txt | awk '{ print $3, $2}' |
2614    egrep '^0x[^01]' | sort -u | perl tag.pl
2615 
2616    where tab.pl is
2617 
2618    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
2619    $n=$first=$last=$idx=0;
2620 
2621    sub fmt {
2622      printf ("\n ") if (($n % 6) == 0);
2623      ++$n;
2624      my($val) = pop(@_);
2625      printf (" \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",", int($val / 256), $val % 256);
2626    }
2627 
2628    while (<>) {
2629      local($ucs,$jis,%rest) = split;
2630      local($u)=hex($ucs);
2631      local($j)=hex($jis);
2632      if ($u - $last > 6) {
2633        if ($last != 0) {
2634          $idx += $last - $first + 1;
2635        }
2636        $first=$u;
2637      } else {
2638        for ($m = $last + 1; $m < $u; ++$m) {
2639      fmt (0);
2640        }
2641      }
2642      fmt ($j);
2643      $last=$u;
2644    }
